    <h3 class="mb-3">Primer: Copilot</h3>
  </hgroup>

  <p data-view-component="true" class="color-fg-muted mb-4">What is Copilot and how do you get started using it? Use this Experience as a Primer on Copilot. We share tutorials, guides and templates to learn how to use AI in your development process.</p>

    <p class="text-normal f5 mb-3">Offers in this bundle</p>
    <ul class="d-flex flex-wrap list-style-none pack__experiences__offers__wrapper pb-2">

  <hgroup role="group" aria-roledescription="Experience Group">
      <p aria-roledescription="subtitle" data-view-component="true" class="color-fg-muted">Tools</p>
    <h3 class="mb-3">Developer Operations</h3>
  </hgroup>

  <p data-view-component="true" class="color-fg-muted mb-4">Developer Operations (DevOps) is the symbiotic relationship between teams, culture and development that allows for collaboration, growth and continuous improvement. Used as a set of practices and tools, DevOps integrates and automates the work of software development and operations as a means for improving the development life cycle.</p>

    <h3 class="mb-3">Intro to GitHub Flow</h3>
  </hgroup>

  <p data-view-component="true" class="color-fg-muted mb-4">GitHub flow is a lightweight, branch-based workflow.  In this Experience you&#39;ll learn the basics of the GitHub Flow including creating and making changes to branches within a repository, as well as creating and merging pull requests. The GitHub flow is useful for everyone, not just developers.</p>

    <h3 class="mb-3">Communicate using Markdown</h3>
  </hgroup>

  <p data-view-component="true" class="color-fg-muted mb-4">Markdown is a lightweight markup language for creating formatted text using a plain-text editor. More simply put, Markdown is a way to write content for the web and one of the most important ways developers can make their communication clear and organized in issues and pull requests. This Experience walks you through the common uses of Markdown in GitHub so that you can feel confident communicating on the platform.</p>

  </div>

  <h4 class="f5">About GitHub Copilot</h4>
  <p class="mb-3">You can use GitHub Copilot to get autocomplete-style suggestions from an AI pair programmer as you code.</p>

  <h4 class="sr-only">Offers</h4>
  <div class="d-flex flex-column mb-3" style="gap: 16px;">
      <div class="color-bg-subtle rounded-2" style="padding: 12px;">
        <h5 class="f5 mb-1">Offer</h5>
        <p style="margin-bottom: 12px;">To enable Copilot, go to your account settings and under Code, planning, and automation, select Copilot. you&#39;ll see &quot;You&#39;re eligible to use copilot for free&quot; and then a button to claim it.</p>
